\lx ʔi
\nep इन्य
\wav vi-Qi
\a i
\ps vi
\ge sulk, get angry
\gn ठुस्किनु
\3s ʔūːtɛ
\xv ʔʌ̄m sʉ̂ːkʌ ʔūːtɛ.
\xn उ कोदेखि ठुस्कियो ।
\xe Who is he angry against?
\xv ʔipɛ ɦʌskolo brâː mʉnɛ muʦɛnʉ.
\xn रिसाएको मान्छेसंग कुरा गर्नु नमीठो हुन्छ ।
\xe It is not nice to discuss with an angry person.
\xv mɛ brâːkʌ ʦʌ̄i ʔûŋ ʔiŋʌtʌ.
\xn त्यो कुरा चाहिं म ठुस्किएँ ।
\xe I got angry from that conversation.
\nq
\dt 08/Oct/2014

\lx ʔiŋ
\nep ऊन्य
\wav vt-QiG
\a iŋ
\ps vt
\ge buy
\gn किन्‍नु
\1s ʔiŋutʌ
\xv ʔuŋʌ tɵpi ʔiŋutʌ. 
\xv ʔuŋʌ ʦʌpdem ʔiŋutʌ.
\xn मैले टोपी किनेँ ।
\xe I bought a cap.
\se ʔiŋ-si
\ps vr
\ge buy for oneself
\gn आफ्‍नो लागि किन्‍नु
\xv ʔûŋ tɵpi ʔunsiŋʌtʌ.
\xn मैले आफ्‍नो लागि टोपी किनेँ ।
\xe I bought a hat for myself.
\nq

\lx ʔʉ
\nep अ्युन्य
\wav vt-Qu
\a u
\ps vt
\ge wake, take care, save
\gn बौराउनु, पालन पोषण गर्नु, बचाउनु
\1s ʔʉŋʌ
\xv ʔuŋʌ reskʌp ʦɵʦʦɵ ʔʉ̂ŋtʌ.
\xn मैले टुहुरो बच्‍चालाई शाला पोषण गरे ।
\xe I took care of an orphan.
\xv ɖʌkʈʌrʔɛ mʌ̂nnɛ khɛppɛ ŋeçpɛ ɦʌs ʔʉtɛ.
\xn डाक्टरले मर्नु लागेको बिरामी बचायो ।
\xe The doctor saved the sick person who was about to die.
\xv titi titi ghoɔ̄lpɛ buplaɦɛm bhɵ̄ːlɛ bhɵ̄ːlɛ ʔʉ̂ŋtʌnu.
\xn सानो चल्‍लाहरुलाई बल्‍ला बल्‍ला बचाएँ ।
\xe We saved the chicks with difficulty.
\se ʔu-si
\wav vr-Qu-si
\ps vr
\ge survive
\gn बाँच्नु
\1e ʔʉ̂nsiŋʌ
\xv ʔûŋ ŋeçpɛ muŋʌtam bhɵ̄ːlɛ bhɵ̄ːlɛ ʔʉ̂nsiŋʌtʌ.
\xn म बिरामी थिएँ बल्‍ला बल्‍ला बाँचेँ ।
\xe As I was sick, I survived with difficulty.
\nq

\lx ʔʉl
\nep अल्न्य
\wav vt-Qul
\wav vt-Qul2
\wav vt-Qul3
\a ul
\ps vt
\ge uproot
\gn उखेल्नु
\1s ʔulu
\1d ʔʉli
\xv gɵ̄ːthɛ jokkilo ɦūːsʌŋ ʔʌ̄lnɛnʌ khoɔ̂nnɛ mʌttʉ.
\xn गोठ सार्दा घोचा उखालेर लानुपर्छ ।
\xe As we move the cowshed, we have to uproot the vertical pole and take it away.
\xv ʦɵʦʦɵpo ŋʌlu ɦʌllei ʦhûː jo ʔʌ̄lkinʌkho nuri ŋʌlu bʌ̄ŋpɛ lʌ̄m.
\xn केटाकेटीको दाँत हल्लिने बित्तिकै उखालेमा नयाँ दाँत राम्रो उम्रिन्छ ।
\xe If we take out the children teeth when they shake, the new teeth grow well.
\xv sʌ̄ŋbi thânpɛ kaʈi ʣʌmʌrʌʔɛ ʔʌ̄lnɛ mʌttʉ.
\xn काठमा ठोकेको काँटी जमराले उखाल्नु पर्छ ।
\xe We have to take out the nails that have been nailed into the wood with a hammer.
\nq revoir husang + jamara

\lx ʔɛt
\nep अ्या:न्‍न्य
\wav vi-Qyat
\a ɛt
\ps vi-t
\ge say
\gn भन्‍नु
\1e ʔɛ̂iŋʌ
\ng Conjugates like an intransitive verb but iʦ agent requires the ergative suffix.
\xv ʔʌ̄mɦɛmʔɛ bʌʣar khoɔçkʌ ʔɛstɛnu.
\xn उनीहरुले बजार जान्छौं भने ।
\xe They said ``We go to the market".
\se ʔɛt-si
\ps vr
\xv ʔɵdi mʉto ʔɛ̂nsi.
\xn बिचार गर्दै भनिन्छ ।
\xe We will be careful of what we say.
\xv mɛʔo ʔɛ̂ntɛsi
\xn मैले त्यसो पो भनेँ ।
\xe Did I say that?
\nq

\lx ʔɛl
\nep अ्याल्न्य
\a ɛl
\ps vt
\ge pull forward
\gn उप्काउनु, ठेल्नु
\1e ʔɛlu
\xv kunabi tɵ̂npɛ kʉ̂r kʌ̄r belabi ʔɛ̄lnɛ mʌttʉ.
\xn कुनामा बिसाएको भारी बोक्दा ठेल्नुपर्छ ।
\xe When one takes a load that was laid on a terrace wall, one has to pull it forward.
\xv ʔʌ̄msuʔɛ ghoɔ̄lpɛ lūŋ gʌ̄lʔɛ ʔɛ̂ltɛsu.
\xn उनिहरूले ठूलो ढुङ्गा गलले पल्टाए ।
\xe They lifted the boulder with a crowbar.
\xv ʔʌsɛ̂l dhuktʌlo sēndi ʔɛ̂ltɛ.
\xn ठेस लाग्दा मेरो नङ उप्कियो ।
\xe My nail came off as I bumped my foot.
\nq

\lx ʔɵtt
\nep अ्वा:न्‍न्य
\wav vt-Qott
\a ott
\ps vt
\ge bring back
\gn फर्काउनु
\xv ʔuŋʌ ʔûː ʣhoŋulo goru ʔoɔttu.
\xn मैले बारी जोत्‍दा गोरु फर्काउछु ।
\xe When I plough fields, I make the ox turn around.
\se ʔɵtt (sɛt)
\ge take revenge
\gn साटो फर्काउनु
\xv jakki brâːbi sɛt ʔoɔnnɛ munʉ.
\xn सानो कुरामा साटो फेर्नु हुँदैन ।
\xe It is not good to take revenge for small matters.
\se ʔɵtt-si
\ps vr
\ge return something for oneself
\gn आफ्‍नो लागि फर्काउनु
\xv ʔuŋ bɛjoŋ ʔoɔ̂nsiŋʌtʌ.
\xn मेरो लागि काँगियो फर्काएँ ।
\xe I returned the comb for myself (I left other things in some place but I brought back the comb)
\nq

\lx ʔɵr
\nep अ्वार्न्य
\a or
\ps vt

\gn मकै भाँच्नु
\1s ʔoru
\1d ʔɵri
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ mʌkʌi ʔɵ̂rtɛ.

\lx kɛl
\nep क्याल्न्य
\wav vt-kyal
\a ɛl
\ps vt
\1s kɛlu
\1d kɛli
\ge cluster together, wear one's hair in a bun
\gn गुजुल्ट्याउनु, चुल्ठी बाँध्नु
\xv bhokoɔr mosʔɛ golɖo kɛ̂ltɛ.
\xn रुख भालुले खराने गुजुल्ट्यायो ।
\xe The bear (climbed the tree and) clustered all branches together (to make a place for him to rest).
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ ʔudhōːsʌm ʦulʈho kɛ̂ltɛnʌ kɛ̄m mʉtɛ.
\xn उसले कपाल चुल्ठी बाँधेर काम गर्‍यो ।
\xe She wore her hair into a bun and worked.
\xv ʔuʔûːbi woŋâmʔɛ sʌ̄ŋ ghas mʌrʌ̄inɛpo lagi ʔʌ̄mʔɛ mʌ̄nʦʌp kɛ̂ltɛ.
\xn उस्को बारीमा अरुले घास दाउरा नकाट्नाको लागि उसले चुल्ठो बाँध्यो ।
\xe He attached the planʦ (in the shape of women's hair as a sign) so that people do not cut plants from his fields.
\xv ʣɛkoɔ̄i mʌtnije ʔɛ̂nnɛʔɛ dephu was nērnʌ ʣɛlʌm kɛ̂lnu.
\xn अन्‍नबाली सप्रियोस भनी उभौली भूमे सकेपछि ज्यलम् पूजिन्छ ।
\xe In order to get good crops, they perform the Jyalam ceremony after the Waas festival.

\xn कोदोको ढीँडो मस्काएर धेरै बेरसम्म बफाएको नरम हुन्छ ।
\xe If we steam the millet porridge for a long time after having stirred it, it becomes soft.
\se kɛl-si
\ps vr
\wav vr-kyal-si

\dt 23/Jul/2013

\lx khekt
\nep खे:न्य
\wav vt-khekt
\a ekt
\ps vt
\ge hang
\gn झुण्ड्याउनु
\1s khektu
\1d kheki
\xv ʔuŋʌ mʌkʌi pūnʣʌtʉ khektu.
\xn म सराङमा मकै झुण्ड्याउँछु ।
\xe I hang corn on the rack over the oven.
\xv ʔīːʦiʔɛ gɵ kheki.
\xn हामीले लुगा झुण्ड्याउँछौं ।
\xe We hang the clothes.
\nq

\lx khemt
\nep खेम्‍न्य
\wav vt-khemt
\a emt4
\ps vt-i
\ge be clumsy, break anything one touches
\gn कुनै पनि वस्तु (कसैको हातमा) नटिक्‍नु
\ng normally used in inverse negative forms
\1e mʌkhēmŋʌ
\xv ʔʌ̄m mâŋʔɛjo mukhēmdʉ.
\xn उस्को हातमा केहि पनि टिक्दैन ।
\xe He breaks anything he touches. (Nothing lasts in his hands)
\xv ʔûŋ mâŋʔɛjo mʌkhēmŋʌ.
\xn मेरो हातमा केहि पनि टिक्दैन ।
\xe Nothing lasts in my hands.
\nq

\dt 24/Feb/2013

\lx khɛtt
\nep ख्या:न्‍न्य
\wav vt-khyatt
\a ɛtt
\ps vt
\ge block, squeeze into (as in a door)
\gn थुन्‍नु, च्याप्‍नु
\xv ku khɛçsʌ dhi mʉ̂npɛ gɵ.
\xn पानी थुनेर पोखरी बनाएको छ ।
\xe A pond was formed by blocking the water.
\xv balibi bʌ̂i mʌwōːnɛpo lagi lɛ̄m khɛ̂npɛ gɵ.
\xn बालीमा गाई नपस्‍नको लागि बाटो थुनेको छ ।
\xe The path is blocked so that the cow cannot go into the crops.
\xv ʦɵʦʦɵpo ʔukhʌ̄r laskʌʔɛ khɛttɛnʌ koɔ̄r ʦhʉktɛ.
\xn बच्‍चाको हात ढोकाले च्यापेर घाउ भयो ।
\xe The child's hand got wounded being trapped in the door.
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ ʔûː ʣhɵ̄ːŋʉlo ʔuʦhēu ʦhīːmʉ mʌnʌ ʔukuna khɛttʉ.
\xn उसले राम्ररी छेउकुना बारी जोत्छ ।
\xe While he ploughs field, he ploughs nicely from the first row up to the terrace wall.
\se khɛtt-si
\wav vr-khyatt-si
\ps vr
\ge be blocked
\gn थुनिनु
\3s khɛ̂ntɛsi
\xv ku khɛ̂ntɛsi.
\xn पानी थुनिएको छ ।
\xe Water accumulated.
\nq

\wav vi-khot

\a ot
\ps vi
\ge go
\gn जानु
\1e khoɔ̂iŋʌ

\xe I went to see the house.
\xv ʔûŋ kʌleʣ khoɔ̂iŋʌ.
\xn म कलेज जान्छु ।
\xe I go to college.
\xv ʔʌ̄m phʌrʌm khɛ̂i mʉkbi dorphu bʌʣar khɵstɛ.
\xn उ अदुवा बेच्न दोर्फु बजार गयो ।
\xe He went to Dorphu bazaar to sell ginger.

\xn उ किताप किन्‍न पसल गयो ।
\xe He went to the bookshop to buy books.
\se2 dûː khoɔ̂nnɛ
\ge ADD GLOSS
\xv ʔʌnɵ̂l rɵ̂ː jâː mʉnɛ dûː khɵstɛ.
\xn आज धान रोप्‍ने मेलो सर्‍यो ।

\nq

\gn नीद्रा नलाग्नु

\1d ghɛri
\xv ʔʌnɵ̂l senɛ ghɛrʌtʌ.
\xn आज राती नीद्रा लागेन ।
\xe I could not sleep last night.
\nq

\lx ghɵm
\nep घ्वाम्‍न्य
\wav vt-ghom
\a om
\ps vt
\ge block the way (and lead to another direction, of animals)
\gn छेक्‍नु
\1s ghomu
\1d ghɵmi
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ phɵ ghoɔ̄msʌ khoɔttɛ.
\xn उसले कुखुरालाई छेक्दै लग्यो ।
\xe He blocked the way of the chicken and lead it away.
\ue With lɵ  ``soul" as its object, this verb is used to refer to a type of death ritual.
\xv ʔʌ̄m mistɛnʌ sak ɦʌptʌbi ʔulɵ ghɵ̂mtɛnu.
\xn ऊ बितेको दुईहप्‍तामा उस्को अन्तिम संस्कार गरे ।
\xe After two weeks of his passing away they performed his final death ritual.
\nq

\wav vt-pott3
\wav vt-pott4
\wav vt-pott5
\a ott
\ps vt
\ge tie, bloom, go moldy
\gn बाँध्नु, कस्‍नु, फुल्नु ढुसी पर्नु
\1s poɔttu
\1d pɵʦi
\xv sāŋloʔɛ khlêːp poɔttɛ.
\xn उसले साङलोले कुकुर बाँध्यो ।
\xe He tied the dog with a chain.
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ thoɔpruʔɛ kʌmbʌrbîm ʔugɵ poɔttɛ.
\xn उसले पटुकाले कम्बरको लुगा बाँध्यो ।
\xe He tied his clothes on his waist with a belt.
\xv gɵ̄ːthɛ mʉkilo tērʔɛ ʦhēlmɛ poɔ̂nnɛ mʌttʉ.
\xn गोठ बनाउँदा चोयाले चित्रो बाँध्नुपर्छ ।
\xe When we make a cowshed, we have to tie the matt with bamboo threads.
\xv ʔaru poɔttʉlo tappo kʌ̄m mʌ̄mki, dhɛrʉ poɔttʉlo ʦēlpɛ kʌ̄m mʌ̄mki.
\xn आरु फुल्दा आफ्नो घर सम्झिईन्छौं, पैयुँ फुल्दा माइती घर संझिन्छौं । (आरु फुल्यो घर, पैयुँ फुल्यो माईता)
\xe When the plum blooms, we miss our home, when the wild cherry blooms, we miss our relatives' house.
\xv thūːnɛmbi bʌ̄ŋpɛ taktibuŋ poɔttɛ.
\xn जङ्गलमा राम्रो लालिगुँरास फुल्यो ।
\xe Nice rhododendrons bloomed in the forest.
\xv kɛpbi tɵ̂npɛ khɛlkhɛ̂m poɔttɛ.
\xn भाँडामा राखिएको जाँडको छोक्रा फुल्यो ।
\xe There are beer dregs in the pot.
\xv thoʦi nuri ɦɵlo ʣhes poɔttʉnʌ ʔoɔ̄m-ʔoɔm ʦhûː.
\xn शरद ऋतु आउँदा लेक फुलेर पहेलम्म्य हुन्छ ।
\xe When the autumn comes, the highlands turns yellow.
\xv ʔʌ̄msupo sʉ̂r poɔttɛ.
\xn उनीहरुको विवाह भयो ।
\xe The got married.
\nq

\lx prekt
\nep प्रे:न्य
\wav vt-prekt
\wav vt-prekt2
\wav vt-prekt3
\a ekt
\ps vt
\ge slap
\gn झापड हान्‍नु
\ge sparkle, blast, sprinkle
\gn उछिट्टिनु
\1e prektu
\xv jʌkʌ̂m prekte.
\xn उस्लाई झापड हान ।
\xe Slap him!
\xv mi prektʉ.
\xn आगो उछिट्टिन्छ ।
\xe The fire sparks.
\xv ʔʌgɵbi ɦilo prektʉ.
\xn मेरो लुगामा हिलो उछिट्टिन्छ ।
\xe Mud sprinkles my clothes.
\xv gipsi noɔ̄mʔɛ ghɵ̂ŋtɛlo prekkhʌtɛ.
\xn घामले सुक्दा भटमास उछिटिन्छ ।
\xe When the sun heats soyabeans, the pod breaks open.
\nq

\lx plʉt
\nep प्ल:न्‍न्य
\wav vt-plut
\a ut
\ps vi
\ge go off (of skin, of rope used to attach an animal to a pole)
\gn खुइलिनु
\ps vt
\ge skin (animal), take off (a hat)
\gn खुइलिनु
\1s pludu
\1d plʉʦi
\xv ɦʌçpɛ kuʔɛ khʌ̄r plʉstɛ.
\xn उमालेको पानीले हात खुइलियो ।
\xe The boiling water skined off his hand.
\xv ʔʌsɛ̂l lūŋbi dhuktʌnʌ ʔʌsēndi plʉstɛ.
\xn ढुङ्गामा ठेस लागेर खुट्टाको नङ फुत्क्यो ।
\xe My leg bumped into a stone and my nail came off.
\xv bʌ̂iʔɛ kilokʌ ribʌ plʉ̂ːtkhʌtɛnʌ bali kʉtɛ.
\xn गाईले किलोबाट डोरी फुत्काएर बाली खायो ।
\xe The cow took off the rope from the pole and ate the crops.
\xv bʌʦhʌʔɛ ribʌ plʉ̂ːtkhʌtɛnʌ ʔumɛ̂mpo dʉt tʉ̂ŋkhʌtɛ.
\xn बाछाले डोरि फुत्काएर त्यस्को माउको दुध खायो ।
\xe The calf took off the rope and drunk its mother's milk.
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ ʔutɵpi plʉ̂ːtɛ.
\xn उसले टोपी फुकाल्यो ।
\xe He took off his hat.
\se plʉt-si
\wav vr-plut-si
\wav vr-plut-si2
\ps vr
\xv ʔubhrēːnɛʔɛ kɛ̄mkʌ plʌ̂ntɛsi.
\xn अल्छिले उ कामबाट फुत्क्यो ।
\xe Because of his lazyness, he took off from his work.
\xv bhêi ʔukâːbikʌ plʌ̂ntɛsi.
\xn सर्पले काचुली फेर्‍यो ।
\xe The snake moulded.
\nq

\lx ɦɵt
\nep ह्वा:न्‍न्य
\wav vi-hot
\a ot
\ps vi
\ge collapse
\xn भत्किनु
\ps vt
\ge cause to collapse
\xn भत्काउनु
\4s ɦoɔ̂i
\xv jʉnɛmbi kanla ɦɵstɛ.
\xn वर्षामा कान्ला भत्क्यो 
\xe The terrace wall collapsed during the monsoon.
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ nʌja lɛ̄m bʌnei mʉnɛpo lagi purano lɛ̄m ɦɵ̂ːtɛ.
\xn उसले नयाँ बाटो बनाउनलाई पुरानो बाटो भत्कायो ।
\xe He destroyed the old trail to make a new trail.
\xv jʉnɛmbi kōːro ɦɵstɛ.
\xn वर्षामा पहिरो गयो ।
\xe There was a landslide during the monsoon.
\se2 ɦoɔ̂nsenɛ
\wav vt-hont-se
\wav vt-hont-se2
\ps vt
\ge pant, be out of breath
\gn स्वाँ स्वाँ गर्नु
\1s ʔiɦoɔ̂iseŋʌ
\1d ʔiɦɵsseʦi
\4s ɦoɔssedʉ
\xv ʔʌ̄m ʔɛnɛke ŋɛstɛlo mʌri ɦoɔssetɛ.
\xn उ बिरामी हुँदा धेरै स्वाँ स्वाँ गर्‍यो
\xe A few days ago he was sick and panted a lot.
\xv rogi goru ʔûː ʣhōŋkilo mʌri ɦoɔssedʉ.
\xn रोगी गोरु बारी जोत्दा धेरै स्वाँ स्वाँ गर्छ
\xe When we plough fields with a sick ox, it pants a lot.
\xv ʣhēːstʉ lɛ̄mthikilo ʔiɦoɔçseki.
\xn लेकमा हिँड्दा स्वास बढ्छ ।
\xe We pant a lot when we walk in the highlands.
\nq

\lx ɦɵnt
\nep ह्वाइन्य
\wav vt-hont
\wav vt-hont2
\wav vt-hont-sa
\wav vt-hont-sa2
\a ont
\ps vt
\ue used in collocations.
\1s ɦoɔ̄ndu
\1d ɦɵ̄ːʦi
\xv nokʦhoʔɛ koɔ̄m ɦoɔ̂ntɛ.
\xn धामीले मूख खोल्यो ।
\xe The shaman practiced an enchantment for the first time (in his life).
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ ʔusôm ɦoɔ̂ntɛ.
\xn उसले श्‍वास फेर्‍यो ।
\xe He drew a deep breath.
\xv ʔʌtēm rɵ̂ː ɦoɔ̂ntɛ.
\xn यो साल धान छिमले भयो ।
\xe This year the rice grows stalks but bears no grains.
\se2 ɦoɔ̄isʌnɛ
\ge reveal a secret
\gn कुरा खुस्काउनु, कुरा खुलाउनु
\1e ɦoɔ̂nsʌŋʌ
\1d ɦɵssɵji
\1p ɦoɔ̄isɵki
\xv ʔûŋpo ʔʌmelsêm phikbi khɵstʌlo woŋâmʔɛ ʔʌbrâː ɦoɔ̂nsʉtnu.
\xn मेरो केटी माग्न जाँदा अरुले मेरो कुरा खुलाइदियो ।
\xe As I was on my way to propose my girlfriend, other people revealed my intentions.
\xv tɛ̄m brâː muɦoɔ̂nsʉwɵ.
\xn यो कुरा नखुलाउ ।
\xe Don't tell this secret.
\nq
